Good tint jobs blend the tint to the end of the window edge but the tint application I received at stealth window leaves 1/8-1/4" untinted.

The tint itself is holding up just fine; however, if you're looking for a clean look, I would shop around.</Review>< user>

< Review>
Great job. Long wait.

Timeline
11/5/2020 Contacted and made appointment for an estimate.
12/21/2020 The estimator came
12/28/2020 Signed contract and paid a $1,000 deposit.
12/29/2020 The office manager acknowledged the contract and the deposit and estimated job start date 5/10/2021.
5/8/2021 A worker (Jim) came to mark out job site
5/10/2021 Job started.
5/12/2021 Paid second installment.
5/13/2021 Signed a change order deleting some work that the foreman said was not necessary. This saved us $900.
5/14/2021 Pier work complete and the foundation slab raised. Paid third installment.
5/18/2021 Foam injection complete
5/21/2021 Repaired the hole that was cut in foundation slab to install a pier
5/21/2021 Job finished. Paid last installment.
5/25/2021 Honey Bucket hauled away their portable toilet
6/4/2021 City inspected the job.

Comments
Â· The company has about 100 employees. They are divided into teams of specialists. We dealt with three teams: pier team, foam injection team, and concrete repair team. All teams were fully booked.
Â·  They brought their own power generator and portable toilet.
Â·  Our project involved putting in seven piers, jacking up the foundation slab, and injecting foam.
Â·  The workers did a neat job. They removed our hardwood floor and saved the tiles before cutting up the foundation slab to put in a pier. They also removed our carpet before drilling holes to inject the foam.
Â·  The pier work involved lots of heavy work.
Â·  Many heavy metal pipes were pushed into the ground against the beams of the foundation slab. These are called piers. The foundation beams were then jacked up against the piers until the floor was level.
Â·  According to the foreman, the piers went down 60 feet before they found sufficient resistance.
Â·  The foam had no function in raising the slab. It was injected several days later. According to the foreman, the foam simply filled the void under the slab. It did not support the slab. (An episode in "This Old House" used foam injection alone to raise the floor slab.)
Â·  Our foundation slab was about two inches thick. I was surprised it could support weight with nothing underneath.

Long wait time but they kept their appointments.

The job costed as much as a new Camry but worth it. Lots of skills, equipment, material, and labor went into the job. Definitely not a DIY project.< /Review>

Great experience from beginning to end. Our newly-remodeled (not done by Bay Area Underpinning) kitchen floor was slowly sinking and we were pretty panicked that it would fall through to the foundation below unless we had some work done quickly.

We were able to get an estimate appointment within a day or two. They agreed that the floor was indeed sinking, but assured us that it wasn't going to fall through imminently. <username>Rico Morales</username>< text>
First time having breakfast here & it was great. Lots of choices for breakfast that all looked good. I decided on the Ham & Pineapple Omelette. Before you judge, it just works! It was so good! Tasted like a Ham & pineapple pizza(Tip: get the salsa, it works as the sauce in a pizza lol) All things aside, it was a great unique omelette. My friend had the Bacon, Avocado cheese omelette & it was just as great too. 5 Stars for service as well. We sat out on the patio & we were well taken care of regarding coffee, water & whatever else needed. Our server was very nice & polite & attentive. Overall, on this morning, on this day, it earned 5 Stars. One of Lodi's best kept secrets is now in our breakfast rotation.</text>

< Review>
Grand Opening

Free reusable bag w/ purchase

I'm a big fan & frequent shopper of the Lakewood Grocery Outlet.  When I saw there would be a Grand Opening close by in Long Beach, I knew I had to go.  Pondering whether I should line up and be amongst the first 50 or so to receive Grocery Outlet bucks, I decided not to as I assumed there would be a massive crowd and I didn't want to deal with the stress.  However, I did swing by later on in the day to receive a free reusable bag, and to checkout the various specially priced merchandise.

Bigger & cleaner & friendlier than the Lakewood location, my eyes spied a bunch of steals I had to take home.

Even though the masses came for the Grand Opening, the lines efficiently flowed in an organized fashion.  The young woman working the register made sure to put on the charm on the first day, and I felt welcome & appreciated.

Parking is via a private lot, shared with Huff's and other businesses.

Grocery Outlet Bargain Market never fails to provide savings for yours truly.  I took home 3 jars of Epic duck fat & several packages of smoked salmon, among others.  Unfortunately, this location is further than the Lakewood location, which means I won't be a recurring customer.  But, for those who live locally, this Grocery Outlet Bargain Market is a wonderful addition to the community, providing excellent customer service and low prices on consumables.

Highly recommend!</Review>

He said they had not started yet as they were trying to get a hold of me on the phone.  I never received any calls from them BTW.  He said they had not started because there was a price discrepancy and the total now would be $71.99.  I agreed to the change.

An hour later he called me to say they were done.  I asked him again if they reset the service interval notice on the car and he said they did.  After paying the cashier and started my car, I noticed that the service interval was still on.  I asked them to reset it and they said they already had.  After going back and forth with another service rep, who gave me many bogus reasons about how that was normal, I asked to speak with a manager.
